Trading with small amounts of money is also known as CFD trading. A Contract For Difference (CFD) is a contract between buyer and seller. This involves an agreement that the seller pays the difference between the opening price and the closing price. CFD is an investment instrument with leveraging which enables you as an investor to gain a financial advantage from both rising and falling share prices.
